msg:Crowne Plaza Hotel, Xiangshan, Ningbo Family Resort Hotel
During the holidays, you must take your children to the beach to dig sand~
We chose the Crowne Plaza Hotel in Xiangshan nearby. It is indeed a family hotel suitable for bringing children. Once you check in, you can get a sand digging tool for free at the front desk
Hotel location
Located in Banbianshan, Xiangshan, the hotel is right outside the beach, which is very convenient. You can catch a lot of mini crabs on the beach
The hotel not only has a large outdoor swimming pool, but also a constant temperature indoor swimming pool and a children's playground. You can play indoors during the day and go to the beach in the evening. It is very comfortable and comfortable
About transportation
Self-driving from Hangzhou to Xiangshan, Ningbo (3 hours)
Recommended attractions
Banbianshan, Donghai: The beach is free. Because it is far from the city, there are not many people and it is very quiet. The sand is also fine and soft. It is very suitable for babies to play. Just like its name, half is sea and half is mountain. The scenery is not bad
The hotel's buffet breakfast also has many varieties, and there are many breakfast options, suitable for adults and children and the elderly
The only drawback is that the check-in is too slow on weekends, and I have been waiting in line for a long time

Disadvantages: I hope the hotel's breakfast can be improved a bit, and the variety is slightly less. After all, the price is there, and it has to match, haha!
